<analysis>**original_problem_statement:**
L'utilisateur a initialement demandé un calculateur d'empreinte carbone, qui a évolué vers une application complète avec tableau de bord, gestion de produits, objectifs, et un futur panneau d'administration.

Récemment, l'utilisateur a fourni un backlog détaillé de nouvelles fonctionnalités (FEAT-01 à FEAT-05 et TECH-01). Les tâches suivantes ont été complétées :
1.  **TECH-01**: Nettoyage et assainissement de la base de données des facteurs d'émission et des sous-catégories, avec création d'un script de test d'intégrité.
2.  **FEAT-04**: Implémentation d'un double mode de saisie (guidé Fiche produit vs Saisie directe) pour le Scope 3 Aval.
3.  **FEAT-02**: Implémentation d'un mode Scénario pour permettre la simulation et la comparaison de stratégies de décarbonation.
4.  **FEAT-01**: Ajout d'un tutoriel d'accueil pour les nouveaux utilisateurs avec .

La demande actuelle de l'utilisateur est d'harmoniser le design de toute l'application pour qu'il corresponde au style moderne de l'onglet Résultats du tableau de bord.

**PRODUCT REQUIREMENTS:**
*   **FEAT-01 — Expérience d'onboarding guidé**: Un tutoriel pas-à-pas pour les nouveaux utilisateurs. (Terminé)
*   **FEAT-02 — Mode Scénario sur les exercices**: Permettre la duplication d'exercices en mode scénario pour la simulation, avec comparaison visuelle sur le tableau de bord. (Terminé)
*   **FEAT-04 — Double mode de saisie pour le Scope 3 Aval**: Offrir le choix entre une saisie via une fiche produit structurée ou une saisie directe et simplifiée. (Terminé)
*   **TECH-01 — Assainissement de la base de données**: Auditer, nettoyer et standardiser les données des facteurs d'émission et des sous-catégories, et créer un script de validation. (Terminé)
*   **TÂCHE UI — Harmonisation du Design**: Appliquer le style visuel de l'onglet Résultats (cartes, ombres, couleurs) à l'ensemble des pages de l'application. (En cours)

**User's preferred language**: Français

**what currently exists?**
Une application full-stack (React/FastAPI/MongoDB) avec les fonctionnalités suivantes implémentées et fonctionnelles :
-   **Gestion de Produits Avancée**: Complète et alignée sur le GHG Protocol.
-   **Tableau de Bord Moderne**: Graphiques avancés et fonctionnalités de comparaison.
-   **Nettoyage de Données**: Une base de données de facteurs d'émission assainie, validée par un script de test automatisé ().
-   **Mode de Saisie Flexible (Scope 3)**: Les utilisateurs peuvent choisir entre une saisie détaillée par produit ou une saisie directe pour le Scope 3 Aval.
-   **Mode Scénario**: Les utilisateurs peuvent créer des scénarios what-if à partir d'exercices existants, les nommer, et les superposer sur le graphique de trajectoire dans l'onglet Objectifs pour une analyse comparative.
-   **Sélecteur d'Exercice Hiérarchique**: Le sélecteur principal distingue clairement les exercices réels des scénarios associés, améliorant la clarté de la navigation.
-   **Tutoriel d'Onboarding**: Un guide interactif se lance pour les nouveaux utilisateurs et peut être relancé depuis la barre latérale.

**Code Architecture**


**Key Technical Concepts**
- **Test d'Intégrité Automatisé (Pytest)**: Création d'un script de test dédié pour garantir la qualité et la cohérence des données de référence dans la base de données.
- **Refonte de Composant (React)**: Réécriture complète de  pour passer d'un simple dropdown à un sélecteur hiérarchique à deux niveaux, améliorant l'UX de la sélection de scénarios.
- **Visualisation de Données (Recharts)**: Superposition d'une ligne de scénario sur un graphique en aires existant pour créer un overlay de comparaison visuelle directe.
- **Gestion d'État Globale (React Context)**: Extension du  pour gérer l'état de l'onboarding de l'utilisateur à travers toute l'application.
- **Intégration de Librairie Tiers**: Utilisation de  pour construire un tutoriel utilisateur guidé et interactif.

self = <PreparedRequest [POST]>, url = '/api/auth/login', params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"
            )
E           requests.exceptions.MissingSchema: Invalid URL '/api/auth/login': No scheme supplied. Perhaps you meant https:///api/auth/login?

self = <PreparedRequest [POST]>, url = '/api/auth/login', params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"
            )
E           requests.exceptions.MissingSchema: Invalid URL '/api/auth/login': No scheme supplied. Perhaps you meant https:///api/auth/login?

self = <PreparedRequest [POST]>, url = '/api/auth/login', params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"
            )
E           requests.exceptions.MissingSchema: Invalid URL '/api/auth/login': No scheme supplied. Perhaps you meant https:///api/auth/login?

self = <PreparedRequest [POST]>, url = 'None/api/auth/login'
params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"

self = <PreparedRequest [POST]>, url = '/api/auth/login', params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"
            )
E           requests.exceptions.MissingSchema: Invalid URL '/api/auth/login': No scheme supplied. Perhaps you meant https:///api/auth/login?

self = <PreparedRequest [POST]>, url = '/api/auth/login', params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"
            )
E           requests.exceptions.MissingSchema: Invalid URL '/api/auth/login': No scheme supplied. Perhaps you meant https:///api/auth/login?

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:

self = <PreparedRequest [POST]>, url = '/api/auth/login', params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"
            )

self = <PreparedRequest [POST]>, url = '/api/auth/login', params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"
            )
E           requests.exceptions.MissingSchema: Invalid URL '/api/auth/login': No scheme supplied. Perhaps you meant https:///api/auth/login?

self = <PreparedRequest [POST]>, url = '/api/auth/login', params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"

self = <PreparedRequest [GET]>, url = '/api/categories', params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"
            )
E           requests.exceptions.MissingSchema: Invalid URL '/api/categories': No scheme supplied. Perhaps you meant https:///api/categories?

self = <PreparedRequest [GET]>, url = '/api/units/dimensions'
params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"
            )
